margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Well I have been a ship Captain for nearly 3 decades. When some one wants to give me a valuable present, whether it be a owner, or a charterer, or a shipper, or a consignee , or an agent\u2014the first thing which crosses their blessed minds in to gift me a nice bottle of wine. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>And being a ship Captain, nobody dares insult me and&nbsp;give me cheap wine, unless they want \"double trouble\".</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gNWzU2oN8r4/To7SXPxdE9I/AAAAAAAAG2A/MyX7Qe7c8Ow/s1600/CP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gNWzU2oN8r4/To7SXPxdE9I/AAAAAAAAG2A/MyX7Qe7c8Ow/s400/CP.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Every time I take a flight to join or sign off from a ship ( usually an average of 3 / 4 connecting flights ) I sample what the airline has to offer \u2014 <span style=\"color: red;\">usually \u201cunpleasant \u201c, \u201cout of balance\u201d , \u201coak reeking\u201d , \u201castringent in the finish\u201d , \u201cunstructured tannin \u201c wines originating from \u201climited hang grafted grapes \u201c <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>affected by <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>fruit flies, Phylloxera louse and downy mildew <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span>from France, Italy, California and Australia in tiny bottles ..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-e4JhQlokwgU/To7ShywzV-I/AAAAAAAAG2I/IulvCdiV21Y/s1600/imagesCAESOVBS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-e4JhQlokwgU/To7ShywzV-I/AAAAAAAAG2I/IulvCdiV21Y/s400/imagesCAESOVBS.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A top grade vintage wine goes by refrigerated containers <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>on ships nowadays.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oaJs-_Hgb2o/To7SpZlSk5I/AAAAAAAAG2M/aGh4sB_Z-ss/s1600/mk.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"265\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oaJs-_Hgb2o/To7SpZlSk5I/AAAAAAAAG2M/aGh4sB_Z-ss/s400/mk.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I got introduced to Chilean wine more than 2 decades ago. My ship had been to Chile and we bought some dirt cheap Chilean wine. The moment the crew saw the cost, nobody wanted to drink the wine. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is assumed that all cheap wines are bad. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>But once they had a sip, almost all who knew something about wine , opined that it was fantastic wine.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">My love affair with Chilean wine started from then on. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Now I find that the whole world has woken up to Chilean wine. The wine did not sell abroad, till Jew Domains Barons De Rothschilds in 1988 bought off a 50% stake in the 250 year old Los Vascos Vineyard in the Chilean Colchagua valley. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7-8JjOA6mFI/To7TLzwqJYI/AAAAAAAAG2U/ygIhuyGHFC4/s1600/FJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7-8JjOA6mFI/To7TLzwqJYI/AAAAAAAAG2U/ygIhuyGHFC4/s400/FJ.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Rothschild JACKED UP the prices knowing wine selling is closely related to snobbery. The moment the cost went up the uppity West started warming up to Chilean wine. </span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Rothschild got wine experts from Bordeaux to supervise the viniculture, harvest, maceration and ageing process. They modernized the process for mass production using temperature controlled stainless steel vats, pneumatic presses, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Rothschild has always known ( like Picasso ) how to market their wines and to buy their own wines using anonymous agents , at record breaking prices, to hit the head lines of the wine magazines and breaking news of TV media which their own.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">So, a 1945 Chateau Mouton Rothschild Jerobaom sold at Christie\u2019s auction in 1997 for 114614 US dollars.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Most of the wine tasters are like the art critics who praise Picasso\u2019s dreadful daubings. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Money talks\u2014these wine critics are usually bribed. The only time they fall into deep shit, is when they are told to blindfold and test.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>But <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>they have some sort of magic communications to still beat the system. It is all a big game.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">First of all none of the wine tasters know how the human mechanism of smell and taste works. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>This is the way God made you, you are NOT having special tongues and noses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">NOW LET ME DIGRESS BRIEFLY INTO THE SCIENCE OF SMELLING AND TASTING.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-43GV0NwIXrE/To7QGBlD-ZI/AAAAAAAAG00/4tDXwLGAPQU/s1600/imagesCAWE9G10.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"186\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-43GV0NwIXrE/To7QGBlD-ZI/AAAAAAAAG00/4tDXwLGAPQU/s320/imagesCAWE9G10.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In India since the past 12000 years we have the system of cleaning the tongue by using a sharp scraper every morning immediately after brushing the teeth. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>You will understand what this means only if you do it once and see for yourself the YUCK toxic slime , known in 7000 year old Vedas as Ama, which comes off . </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Rd8yEqcG3YM/To7QKl-LeMI/AAAAAAAAG04/Zo3laSmZy9U/s1600/imagesCAE1YIF7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"384\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Rd8yEqcG3YM/To7QKl-LeMI/AAAAAAAAG04/Zo3laSmZy9U/s400/imagesCAE1YIF7.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is mostly dead tongue taste buds and cells. There are more than 10000 taste buds on your tongue whose life is just 10 days.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-I5PRnZ-QLko/To7QR_depYI/AAAAAAAAG08/QwI6b7oAPj4/s1600/250px-Gray1018.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-I5PRnZ-QLko/To7QR_depYI/AAAAAAAAG08/QwI6b7oAPj4/s400/250px-Gray1018.png\" width=\"389\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It also brings out dead bacteria, fungus , plaque coating, fur, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>bad smelling volatile sulphur compounds and stuck food debris. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Indians were the first to do this and it was introduced to China by Indian Kalari warrior sage Bodhi Dharma .<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The mouths of people who don\u2019t use the tongue scraper stinks. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-y9xi3dJED8c/To7QaCmZMYI/AAAAAAAAG1A/IGFi4Z_drlI/s1600/untitledNNN.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-y9xi3dJED8c/To7QaCmZMYI/AAAAAAAAG1A/IGFi4Z_drlI/s400/untitledNNN.png\" width=\"369\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A girl could be the most beautiful in the world, but if she has repulsive MO, you would not want to kiss her at all. She can chew Wrigley's double mint gum throughout the day, her mouth will still smell like crap\u2014and this is NOT from bad teeth or rotten gums..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-x-fiywruVII/To7RZbdS07I/AAAAAAAAG1k/Yd0Gs_VavBs/s1600/imagesCALO1I2F.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"217\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-x-fiywruVII/To7RZbdS07I/AAAAAAAAG1k/Yd0Gs_VavBs/s320/imagesCALO1I2F.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Clean and healthy taste buds on a unfurred tongue can 1/200 sweet, 1/400 salt and 1/ 135000 sour and 1/2000000 bitter. Contrary to what experts say, taste buds all over the tongue can taste everything\u2014there are no maps.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\nNever confuse taste with flavour. Taste is a chemical sense perceived by the receptor cells in the taste buds. Falvour is a fusion of multiple senses. With spicy food the brain registers pain as one aspect of flavour. To perceive flavour brain interprets taste , smell and other stimuli and sensations.<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The moment the food or drink is smelt the Pavlovian response secretes saliva, preparing the tongue for tasting. Hence odours play an important role in the taste of foods. If you plug your nose you cannot make out the difference between strawberry jam and cherry jam\u2014 for both will taste sweet. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Your perception of scent is more than a thousand times stronger than your perception of taste. Taste is 78% smell. You must pity the guys whose noses are blocked and who breathe in through their mouths. They wont even feel the desire to eat. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--E4roMkyfb0/To7RTk2bAqI/AAAAAAAAG1g/NNme4OUOcXs/s1600/imagesCAIMYDI4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--E4roMkyfb0/To7RTk2bAqI/AAAAAAAAG1g/NNme4OUOcXs/s1600/imagesCAIMYDI4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">We cant see bacteria with your eyes, yet we never eat rotten putrid food as our sense of smell which can detect more than 10000 different odours , warns us in advance. A top quality perfume has more than 450 ingredients.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This is why when you smell the wine you must fill up the glass 25% and swirl the wine and allow it coat the sides of the glass , so that it vapourises and tosses molecules into the air, releasing the bouquet. Sniff first and only then swirl. Sweeter wines will leave thick viscous streaks.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The top part of the glass will give you the floral and fruit odours. Put your nose in and take a big deep sniff to cross the threshold of sensitivity\u2014to get that first impression of the wine before olfactory fatigue sets in after a few seconds. The best time to smell is in the afternoon when both your nostrils are clear and smell membranes sensitive.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before you do that tilt the glass away from you ( or Emily Post will make fun of you <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>) and look at the edge of the liquid against a white tablecloth\u2014to judge hue and clarity. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zbvq-NEjEYo/To7Q7znb0AI/AAAAAAAAG1Q/k4C9IKayQXw/s1600/qwe.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"288\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zbvq-NEjEYo/To7Q7znb0AI/AAAAAAAAG1Q/k4C9IKayQXw/s400/qwe.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Older wines are darker and will have an orange tinge at the edge. We on chemical tankers who do wallwash tests with Methanol are experts in all this.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Now sip up enough wine to swirl and slosh it around in your mouth to that every corner of your tongue , for viscosity and tannins. Allow the wine to settle on your lower mouth and now slurp in air to make the volatile parts travel to the back of your nasal cavity for the aroma. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Swallow and feel the after taste , alcohol content , acidity, and linger. . Inhale retro nasally to give a hit to the five million nerve cells<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-h-y72c2MZgc/To7RBJ4kqQI/AAAAAAAAG1U/NtSFyEEGggM/s1600/as.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"304\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-h-y72c2MZgc/To7RBJ4kqQI/AAAAAAAAG1U/NtSFyEEGggM/s320/as.gif\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">Now remember the best and most famous wine tasters of this planet have been served the same vine from the same bottle and come up with hilarious differences, and branded one as cheap and other a expensive vintage.</span> <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--lq4o2I-O4k/To7RG4X96SI/AAAAAAAAG1Y/Hq4LW-Bzauc/s1600/imagesCABUCQ98.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/--lq4o2I-O4k/To7RG4X96SI/AAAAAAAAG1Y/Hq4LW-Bzauc/s400/imagesCABUCQ98.jpg\" width=\"327\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A little bit of temperature difference can affect the judgement. White wine is always chilled and red wine at room temperature\u2014this means about 18 deg C\u2014NOT 32 deg C like in India. Lower temperatures mute the aromatics . Aromatics get liberated inside the warm mouth. It is through the aroma that the wine is actually tasted. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-c8SkgWbgBno/To7RMacLWeI/AAAAAAAAG1c/a8nyVhyzwDU/s1600/imagesCA6JJRLY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"292\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-c8SkgWbgBno/To7RMacLWeI/AAAAAAAAG1c/a8nyVhyzwDU/s400/imagesCA6JJRLY.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This is different from bouquet which refers to smell from fermentation , exposure to oak, and ageing. Scientists use Gas Chromatograph mass spectrometers to analyse the aromas, as wine makers have started using illegal flavourings. On Chemical tankers we use Gas ion Chromatographs to find the chlorides.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">One of my European Chief Engineers used to tell me how he makes wine in his house when he is on leave, and he would show me pictures. He would put a latex glove on the neck of the vat. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>When the limp glove gets filled with gas and then becomes limp again\u2014that is the time to start drinking. He was firmly convinced that drinking lot of red wine with flavonoids makes you live longer and can prevent heart attack \u2014till I told his that is all bull dished out by the wine-mafia.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chilean wines are good as the grapes in that part of the world is NOT affected by louses and fungi. Chile lies in one corner of the world, totally sanitized by the Andes mountain range. The climate is temperate , due to the cold Humboldt ocean current, and the soil rich in minerals, highly permeable and well draining. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-mtVPY6r0rC0/To7R-TCje7I/AAAAAAAAG14/OSYeBhKyuJ4/s1600/yip.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-mtVPY6r0rC0/To7R-TCje7I/AAAAAAAAG14/OSYeBhKyuJ4/s400/yip.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There is low rainfall , clear sunny skies, hot days and cool nights for colour and aroma , no frost because of unpolluted winds from the Pacific, which again means no fungus and louses. . This means acid, sweet tannins and alcohol are in balance.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ESEqx-PzneY/To7R4PhflsI/AAAAAAAAG10/CEacJxSxQn8/s1600/rr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I love to have a reasonably priced, classic, red <span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">Don Melchor Cabernet Sauvignon </span>( Concha Y Toro ) <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>from the Maipo valley\u2014just because I have visited the place and made a mental connection.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>You will love any Merlot or Carmenere wine with delightful blends of unique flavours and a dash of minerality.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Chocolate, caramalised nuts, strawberry, plums, leather and earth, blackberries, raspberries, cherries, cracked pepper, candy berry, fresh rose, spicy red berry, coconut, olives, figs, marsh mellow, toasted nuts, prunes, pineapple, peaches, lemon curd, banana, apricot, lychee, minty black currant, coffee, custard, exotic herbs</span></em></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">From the evening of Ashtami , the eight day till the morning of the Vijaya Dashami tenth day, we are forbidden from touching our books.&nbsp; One token book would be sent to the the local temple and the rest stacked up in the puja room of the house.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">As a small kid, to impress my vernacular playing friends studying in Malayalam medium schools, I used to cover up the big fat Chambers English dictionary, and include it in my book stack . </span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">And they would all cry WOW!&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So many books !! ( and then they would look at me as if I was THE genius ) </span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-C2spzrVcms4/To3cYLQhnNI/AAAAAAAAG0E/-ATLcMj6Ny8/s1600/imagesCA0F265T.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-C2spzrVcms4/To3cYLQhnNI/AAAAAAAAG0E/-ATLcMj6Ny8/s1600/imagesCA0F265T.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Every body including adults cannot touch their tools on the 9th day ( Maha navami ) Ayudha puja</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is kept for worship on the altar of the divine.   <span style=\"color: black; line-height: 150%;\">If one can make a conscious effort to see the Divine in the tools and objects one uses each day, it will help one to see one's work as an offering to God.</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-O90l1XvbizU/To3cceCANwI/AAAAAAAAG0I/iA6TUm3dsSM/s1600/imagesCAZBUNX2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-O90l1XvbizU/To3cceCANwI/AAAAAAAAG0I/iA6TUm3dsSM/s1600/imagesCAZBUNX2.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This means on the 10th day there will be no newspaper in the morning. The diety is Saraswati, the Goddess of learning.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The 10th auspicious day is called Vijaya Dashimi. On the morning after a bath, the books or tools have to be taken out and used. Both my children at the age of three was initiated into the world of letters on this day morning--after the nine days if Navratri.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The children of 3 or 5 are taken to the temple ( or done in the house ) for the Vidyarambham ceremony, as a unique annual ritual.&nbsp; For this learning initiation the child is made to sit on the lap of the parents or grandparents in front of the picture or statue of Goddess Saraswati.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The mantra </span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\">\"<b>Om Hari Shree Ganapathaye Namah</b>\"(</span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\">\u0d13\u0d02</span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\">\u0d39\u0d30\u0d3f</span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\">\u0d36\u0d4d\u0d30\u0d40</span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\">\u0d17\u0d23\u0d2a\u0d24\u0d2f\u0d47</span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\">\u0d28\u0d2e\u0d03</span><span style=\"background: white; color: black; line-height: 150%;\">) is written on the tongue of the child with a gold ring dipped in honey and vayampu. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"background: white; color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Then the child is made to write the same thing in rice on a flat platter made of bell metal, with the right index finger ,uttering each syllable as it is written--prompted by the elder hand.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"background: white; color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On the 8th , 9th and 10th days thousands throng in Kerala temples.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"background: white; color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">It was on this Vijaya Dashimi day the Pandava brothers ( Mahabharata ) found their weapons after one year incognito. Pandavas were defeated in a gambling game with Kauravas headed by Duryodhana. According to the challenge they were supposed to live in forest for 12 years and as incognito for one year.&nbsp;</span></em></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></em></span></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">During incognito they are were not allowed to carry weapons. </span></em></span><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">For the safety of the weapons they dug a hole under the shami tree and put all the weapons in. When they were back after one year, they were filled with joy to see all the weapons safe at the same place. Our prasadam was Pradhaman payasam made of jaggery.&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">on </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Vijayadashimi day&nbsp;, to read a&nbsp; bit&nbsp; from</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; THEY COME BACK HOME HIGHLY STRESSED .. THE IS NO CATHARSIS PROVIDED BY THROWING STONES ON 3 SHAITANS ( BRAHMA/ VISHNU AND SHIVA )..&nbsp;</span></b><br /><br />IN ANCIENT DAYS IT WAS THREE IDOLS --TODAY REPLACED BY 3 PILLARS.. MOHAMMAD THE PROPHET NEVER SANCTIONED THIS MANDATORY ISLAMIC HAJ RITUAL .. THESE ARE FAKE HADITHS INSERTED BY JEWS..<br /><br />STONING IS NOT PART OF THE HOLY KORAN.. After 22 years , in 1788 Hyder\u2019s son Tipu razed my hometown Calicut again to the ground \u2013 he came with elephants, cannons, rockets and more than 68000 soldiers, via the Sultan Battery ghats..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He renamed all the towns with Islamic names. My hometown Kozhikode became Islamabad. Today only Feroke retains the old name. Rest have all been named back to original. British changed Kozhikode again to Calicut. Today once again it is back to Kozhikode , as my passport bears testimony. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Famous ancient temples looted and desecrated as per British records were : Triprangot, Thrichembaram, Thirunavaya, Thiruvannoor, Calicut Thali, Hemambika Temple, the Jain Temple in Palghat, Mammiyur, Parambatali, Venkitangu, Pemmayanadu, Tiruvanjikulam, Terumanam, Vadakhumnnathan Temple of Trichur, Belur Siva Temple, Shri Veliyanattukava, Varakkal, Puthu, Govindapuram, Keraladhiswara, Trikkandiyur, Sukapuram, Bhagavati temple Kodungallur, Maranehei Temple of Aaalvancheiri Tambrakkal, Vengara Temple of Aranadu, Tikulam, Ramanathakra, Azhinjalam Indiannur, Mannur Narayan Kanniar and Vadukunda Siva Temple of Madai. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 12pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The biggest loss was the 7000 year old Thirunavazha temple, along with priceless Vedic records. This temple was even older than 6000 year old Guruvayur.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tipu Sultan was prevented from destroying the Guruvayur temple by Hydrose Kutty, who told him that the 6000 year old black idol has been shifted to the Ambalapuzha Sri Krishna temple in kingdom of Travancore for safekeeping. Even today, daily pujas are conducted in Ambalapuzha Sri Krishna Temple where the idol of Guruvayoor Temple was temporarily installed and worshipped.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 12pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I have visited the spot Tipu Sultan fell when I was a young boy of 11. At that time I felt sorry for him , for he was mentioned in my social studies and history book of school as a freedom fighter.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-b1LtUzGGHJY/To2LJAgGDgI/AAAAAAAAGzY/l2Q94oIVaHY/s1600/imagesCAXY78S5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-b1LtUzGGHJY/To2LJAgGDgI/AAAAAAAAGzY/l2Q94oIVaHY/s1600/imagesCAXY78S5.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 12pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 12pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>At the spot he had fallen there is a stone memorial , which I had visited, along with his palaces in Srirangapatman- all built with Hindu temple treasures. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DfA1jxpG6jQ/To2K8fZpOZI/AAAAAAAAGzQ/9WuNYLugB2c/s1600/imagesCAD5E2MF.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DfA1jxpG6jQ/To2K8fZpOZI/AAAAAAAAGzQ/9WuNYLugB2c/s1600/imagesCAD5E2MF.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 12pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 2003 the sword of Tipu Sultan was bought by Vijay Mallya for a fortune . font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">QUOTE: Al-Biruni wrote an encyclopedic work on India called \u201cTarikh Al-Hind\u201d (History of India) in which he explored nearly every aspect of Indian life, including religion, history, geography, geology, science, and mathematics. My book is nothing but a simple historic record of facts. I shall place before the reader the theories of the Hindus exactly as they are, and I shall mention in connection with them similar theories of the Greeks in order to show the relationship existing between them.(1910, Vol. 1, p. 7;1958, p. 5)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Hindus considered Muslims violent and impure, and did not want to share anything with him.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Over time, Al-Biruni won the welcome of Hindu scholars. Al-Biruni collected books and studied with these Hindu scholars to become fluent in Sanskrit, discover and translate into Arabic the mathematics, science, medicine, astronomy and other fields of arts as practiced in 11th century India. He was inspired by the arguments offered by Indian scholars who believed earth must be ellipsoid shape, with yet to be discovered continent at earth's south pole, and earth's rotation around the sun is the only way to fully explain the difference in daylight hours by latitude, seasons and earth's relative positions with moon and stars.[36] Al-Biruni was also critical of Indian scribes who he believed carelessly corrupted Indian documents while making copies of older documents.[37] Al-Biruni's translations as well as his own original contributions reached Europe in 12th and 13th century, where they were actively sought.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">CONTINUED TO 2--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">CONTINUED FROM 1--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">While others were killing each other over religious differences, Al-Biruni had a remarkable ability to engage Hindus in peaceful dialogue. Mohammad Yasin puts this dramatically when he says, \u201cThe Indica is like a magic island of quiet, impartial research in the midst of a world of clashing swords, burning towns, and burned temples.\u201d (Indica is another name for Al-Biruni\u2019s history of India). Al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b accomplished most of his work in the period between 813 and 833. After the Muslim conquest of Persia, Baghdad became the centre of scientific studies and trade, and many merchants and scientists from as far as China and India traveled to this city, as did al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b. He worked in Baghdad as a scholar at the House of Wisdom established by Caliph al-Ma\u2019m\u016bn, where he studied the sciences and mathematics, which included the translation of Greek and Sanskrit scientific manuscripts.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b's Z\u012bj al-Sindhind[11] (Arabic: \u0632\u064a\u062c \u0627\u0644\u0633\u0646\u062f \u0647\u0646\u062f\u200e, \"astronomical tables of Sindh and Hind\") is a work consisting of approximately 37 chapters on calendrical and astronomical calculations and 116 tables with calendrical, astronomical and astrological data, as well as a table of sine values. This is the first of many Arabic Zijes based on the Indian astronomical methods known as the sindhind.[22] The work contains tables for the movements of the sun, the moon and the five planets known at the time. This work marked the turning point in Islamic astronomy. Hitherto, Muslim astronomers had adopted a primarily research approach to the field, translating works of others and learning already discovered knowledge.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; As the name suggests when heated, this material may evolve killer toxic cyanide gas, or explode, or both.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; Do 5 times at 15 sec intervals.<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Uses: nitrile rubber, grain fumigant, acrylic fibre, plastics, luggage , dinnerware<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">DO NOT use dry chemical for large, confined fire. If the tank is fitted with an N2 line, a fire may be extinguished by introducing N2. Water or foam may cause frothing. Keep tank cool with water spray. Fire-fighters must wear respiratory protection and full protective clothing including rubber boots.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Moderate irritating volatile chemicals, such that personnel will not usually tolerate moderate or high vapor concentrations.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Minimum hazards. Usually includes chemical which, if spilled on clothing and allowed to remain, will cause smarting and reddening of the skin with blisters and erythema. Wash with soap and flush with water.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Always use goggles.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Odor threshold (ppm)/ 21.4<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Permissible exposure limits/TWA/ 29 ppm<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Threshold limit value/TWA/ 2 ppm<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Harmful by inhalation and skin absorption. Penetrates leather, liquid in shoes causes delayed bums. Contaminated leather shoes and gloves should be destroyed.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Eye irritation, headache, nausea, blueness of lips and finger tips. Contact with skin may also cause dermatitis.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">STEL/ 400 ppm for 30 minutes<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Penetrates leather. Contaminated leather gloves must be destroyed. Use butyl rubber gloves.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Inhibitor is MEHQ about 44ppm.(ethyl hydroquinone )/ 4 methoxy phenol (these are oxygen dependant, so do NOT inert tank )<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Use PPE of PVC, neoprene, HD polyethylene<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Remove victim to fresh air. If he is not breathing, apply artificial respiration. Remove contaminated clothing and wash chemical from skin with gentle flow of water. Get medical attention. If patient is unconscious, administer vapor of amyl nitrite (Break an Amyl Nitrite ampoule in a cloth and hold it lightly under the nose of the victim, but away from the person giving first aid, for about 15 seconds. Repeat five times at about 15 second's intervals).<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Very reactive; may polymerize explosively in the presence of strong bases (such as caustic soda). The product must be inhibited to prevent polymerization. Polymerization could be initiated by visible light.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Copper and copper alloys are attacked and should not be used. Attacks aluminum in high concentrations Aluminum, Magnesium, Zinc, galvanized steel and Lithium should not come in contact with Acrylonitrile .<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Materials normally used in electrical apparatus, such as copper, aluminum and insulation, should as far as practicable be protected to prevent contact with the vapor of Acrylonitrile.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Group 15. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>See also exceptions to the chart<b> </b><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">(Do not stow adjacent to Caustic).<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Wear rubber gloves, breathing apparatus, protective clothing. Avoid contact with liquid.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If leak on cargo transfer system, stop the transfer and empty the line system. Secure ignition sources. Flush contaminated area with a weak LAC solution (1%), then flush the area with large quantities of water.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Ensure inhibitor certificate is on board prior loading.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"FR2\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Chemical incompatibility Acrylonitrile/ Caustic soda solution<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"FR4\" style=\"margin: 7pt 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Experience has shown that there is danger of hazardous reaction between Acrylonitrile (group 15) and Caustic soda solution (group 5). This combination is considered compatible for adjacent stowage by current regulations (46 CFR part 160). While a review of the data used to construct the compatibility chart in these regulations showed no reactivity between these two chemicals at test temperatures up to 100 \u00b0C, the new data indicates that a delayed reaction may occur, which generates large amounts of heat if the mixture is vigorously stirred. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"FR3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">DO NOT LOAD ACRYLONITRILE ( GROUP 15 ) AND CAUSTIC SODA ( GROUP 5 ) SOLUTION IN ADJACENT TANKS, AS AN EXCEPTION TO USCG COMPATIBILITY CHART.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Acrylonitrile is an unstable product when not inhibited. Acrylonitrile is regulated for bulk transportation by the IMO, BCH and IBC codes. Following is the summary of the codes' minimum requirements:<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"></span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Alcohol resistant foam<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-x4mKNEy1Ots/TobnZiZ1_9I/AAAAAAAAGt8/doyoW1MmRCE/s1600/imagesCADPHS87.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-x4mKNEy1Ots/TobnZiZ1_9I/AAAAAAAAGt8/doyoW1MmRCE/s1600/imagesCADPHS87.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span><strong>REMOVAL OF ACRYLONITRILE FROM DRIP TRAYS<o:p></o:p></strong></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Any product that may enter drip trays when disconnecting the cargo hoses must be transferred to a slop tank or a toxic waste container by safe methods. Personnel must wear rubber gloves, face shield, plastic coated clothing and wear self-contained breathing apparatus. Small spills may be flushed away with water.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For washing: give cold prewash and then a hot wash.</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;
