margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">TRUMAN CAPOTE</span>- <span style=\"color: blue;\">THE NOVELIST WHO SOLD HIS SOUL</span>\u2014 <span style=\"color: magenta;\">CLASSIC MASTER PIECE AND TRAIL BLAZING NOVEL</span> --</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"background-color: purple; color: yellow; font-size: x-large;\">\u201c IN COLD BLOOD\u201d</span> <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GR9d1EgTIb0/TobTmelDIpI/AAAAAAAAGrA/Bc7WbGwueGY/s1600/498px-TrumanCapote1959.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GR9d1EgTIb0/TobTmelDIpI/AAAAAAAAGrA/Bc7WbGwueGY/s400/498px-TrumanCapote1959.jpg\" width=\"332\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I read the non-fiction true account book IN COLD BLOOD , by American author Truman Capote at the tender age of 11. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I had just come out of the Enid Blyton stage , and this was my first big novel. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This book was in my school library and I was impressed by the fact that it got rave reviews and sold half a million copies in the first two weeks after it was published. To be frank this book should be banned from school libraries.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Since then I got several opportunities to read this book again, but something inside me stopped me every time . Much later in life , I got hold of a E-book copy. I still hold this in my pen drive, but have never read this.&nbsp; At the same time I should say categorically - Capote has breathed in such realism into this superbly crafted&nbsp;classic, that it can&nbsp;hardly be&nbsp;surpassed ever.</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Three years ago I saw the Hollywood movie Capote by DVD while at sea.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Truman Capote is acted out by Phillip Seymour Hoffman, who made the character come alive\u2014and how!.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gY3y7m4VDns/TobT0rix7DI/AAAAAAAAGrE/6lITPWKz0-8/s1600/220px-Capote_Poster.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gY3y7m4VDns/TobT0rix7DI/AAAAAAAAGrE/6lITPWKz0-8/s400/220px-Capote_Poster.jpg\" width=\"300\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Hoffman <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>truly deserved whatever accolades came his way, including 2006 academy award and Globe award for best actor. Looks to me that he was born to do this once in a lifetime role, to portray a openly gay and attention craving complex character, with a high pitched voice and grotesque mannerisms ..the ultimate consummate self publicist. It is NOT an easy role to do justice to.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hEsgFohWVo4/TobT6ZuFzVI/AAAAAAAAGrI/Tn0AypVOjsA/s1600/capote_seymour_184_1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hEsgFohWVo4/TobT6ZuFzVI/AAAAAAAAGrI/Tn0AypVOjsA/s400/capote_seymour_184_1.jpg\" width=\"274\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The shallow thinking common Yank has NOT figured out what happened at Herb Clutter\u2019s ranch in Holcomb.&nbsp; Two drifters , out on parole murder Herb Clutter, his wife Bonnie and his two teenaged children Nancy and Kenyon. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Capote biased approach in the book paints<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Perry Smith as the wronged angel, and portrays the other man Dick Hickock as a diabolical killer. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-pRpZQJRh1SM/TobVACFNBbI/AAAAAAAAGrQ/4Ze3m6AqztM/s1600/imagesCA22FFSR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"286\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-pRpZQJRh1SM/TobVACFNBbI/AAAAAAAAGrQ/4Ze3m6AqztM/s400/imagesCA22FFSR.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If you are objective as a crime detective, or even a journalist , it is simple to see that all shootings and throat slittings were done by Perry, the homosexual. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Dick has NOT killed anybody, though it is claimed that he was the brains behind the would be robbery of a safe which always held more than 10000 dollars, that went awry.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is common knowledge that Truman Capote went regularly to jail for 5 years , to have a tete e tete<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>and sex with Perry, facilitated by lead detective Alvin Dewey , whose wife was a great fan of Capote. Capote bribed the jail warden too. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He was indeed in true love with killer Perry and this small village in Kansas in the heartland of America had just 250 inhabitants, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>probably with NIL homosexuals to give him release while on the job.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Joseph John Maloney, a convicted murderer , on his release in 1972, had spilled the beans. Both Perry and Dick were homosexual partners in prison. JJ Maloney became an investigative reported at Kansas City Star, and he was nominated for Pulitzer prize 5 times. He says that Dick was hetero-sexual, and probably had a homosexual relationship in jail with Perry , usual in American prisons , where there are no women.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">JJ said that Dick tried to rape the attractive 16 year old Nancy Clutter. In a fit of gay jealousy passive gay partner Perry did the shootings and the throat slittings, to show that he is a man\u2019s man.. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Dick\u2019s role was to attempt to rob them after tying and gagging the victims. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">Just before Perry was hanged he kissed Truman Capote on the cheek, and Capote fled tears streaming, without waiting to watch the hanging </span>. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He stood stoically and <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>watched Dick hanging, just before that.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The reason why Capote had a relationship with Perry , who was in prison was two fold. This is where I say that he sold his soul. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He extracted maximum juice by way of classified information about the killings, from Perry \u2013getting him to feel that a famous man like Capote had the clout to delay the hangings. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">And the diabolical <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>part is that Truman Capote delayed releasing his book till both Dick and Perry were hanged.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">Dead men tell no tales, after reading no book, right?</span> <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The book brought Capote fame and riches, and more importantly a guaranteed top perch in the American literary canon, but no peace of mind.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>He wasted his life on drink and drugs , and did not write any other novel, till he died in 1984 at the age of 59, though he was so gifted in playing around with words.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"No one will ever know what In Cold Blood took out of me,\" Capote once said.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>\"It scraped me right down to the marrow of my bones. It nearly killed me. I think, in a way, it did kill me.\"&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">Why not?<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Such poor ethics,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>where he USED a lover on the death row, incapable of defending himself, -- a man, who had put his full trust in him and reposed in him , his entire faith.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This book which was the first attempt to merge journalism with novelistic devices , to create a new literary art form -- is dishonest to the core.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Think over what I said. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Now I shall talk about the gripping book IN COLD BLOOD\u2014a non-fiction book , which sold half a million copies in the first week ( something hard to beat ) . It is now available in 30 languages. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-78R3m9dPNRk/Tobc9Mok1uI/AAAAAAAAGtc/iQ3aVvnoTc8/s1600/imagesCA1SHUHX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-78R3m9dPNRk/Tobc9Mok1uI/AAAAAAAAGtc/iQ3aVvnoTc8/s400/imagesCA1SHUHX.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Check out the extravagant and evocative prose of the opening page --<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">\u201cThe village of Holcomb stands on the high wheat plains of western Kansas, a lonesome area that other Kansans call \"out there.\".<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The local accent is barbed with a prairie twang, a ranch-hand nasalness, and the men, many of them, wear narrow frontier trousers, Stetsons, and high-heeled boots with pointed toes.&nbsp; The land is flat, and the views are awesomely extensive; horses, herds of cattle, a white cluster of grain elevators rising as gracefully as Greek temples are visible long before a traveler reaches them\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Now check out how he finished his book- <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">\"And nice to have seen you, Sue. Good luck,\"&nbsp; he called after her as she disappeared down the path, a pretty girl in a hurry, her smooth hair swinging, shining - &nbsp;just such a young woman as Nancy might have been.&nbsp; Then, starting home, he walked toward the trees, and under them, leaving behind him the big sky, the whisper of wind voices in the wind-bent wheat\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gc_RaECIDCs/TobbGTQfsPI/AAAAAAAAGtM/FAz2cupv-y4/s1600/imagesCABCIT5T.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"234\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gc_RaECIDCs/TobbGTQfsPI/AAAAAAAAGtM/FAz2cupv-y4/s400/imagesCABCIT5T.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The story has a fictionalized ending with a visit of Susan , Nancy\u2019s friend to the Garden City graveyard ,&nbsp; 4 years after<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the Clutters were laid to rest, when detective Dewey bumps into her .&nbsp; Life goes on\u2014 it comes full circle\u2014 cries have become whispers<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">This extraordinary sangfroid <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>, playing around with the nuances , is what makes the book so haunting\u2014the work of a genius.</span> <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-16K5Vl85zuw/TobZlGj-34I/AAAAAAAAGs4/2wnPaBZ17Dw/s1600/imagesCA15HEFN.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-16K5Vl85zuw/TobZlGj-34I/AAAAAAAAGs4/2wnPaBZ17Dw/s400/imagesCA15HEFN.jpg\" width=\"337\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The readers know the outcome of the book right from the start, yet Capote manages to build suspense. Capote allows characters to tell their own story, in a seamless manner, creating a relationship between the reader, the killers ,the victims\u2014literally all, whipping up sympathy for the wrong guy. Readers feel empathy for Perry, the gruesome killer. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pY2dFb_raQk/TobZUjzjoTI/AAAAAAAAGs0/yEg69QJXbbs/s1600/imagesCALVHYA1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pY2dFb_raQk/TobZUjzjoTI/AAAAAAAAGs0/yEg69QJXbbs/s400/imagesCALVHYA1.jpg\" width=\"269\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He tries to make Perry , his gay partner for 5 long years smell of roses all the while. On the other hand he runs down Dick at the drop of a hat and it is clear that he has no time for him. Dick is portrayed as a child rapist , a cold hearted , hard core criminal without a moral compass, and a cruel man who deliberately drives over dogs\u2014all figments of his skewed imagination. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bQn0Tb4C-Ro/TobY_UBSq-I/AAAAAAAAGso/ooWaMI0P78k/s1600/imagesCA5HHTSK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bQn0Tb4C-Ro/TobY_UBSq-I/AAAAAAAAGso/ooWaMI0P78k/s400/imagesCA5HHTSK.jpg\" width=\"269\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">According to him Perry was in jail just because of Dick.&nbsp; Dick Hickock's face was \"composed of mismatching parts . . . as though his head had been halved like an apple, then put together a fraction off center'\u2019.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-g6M3KxlBlz8/TobZF9hCu1I/AAAAAAAAGss/KI9Q-3JCYKg/s1600/imagesCA6XEU27.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>While Smith\u2019s stocky weight lifter's torso with dainty feet that \"would have neatly fitted into a delicate lady's dancing slippers\" .&nbsp; Probably he had a footsie gay fetish .&nbsp; Capote tells Harper Lee , that when he first saw Perry he found his puppy dog eyes irresistible and found his short dangling legs ( injured in a motor bike accident ) hanging off a chair without touching the floor absolutely charming. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Tjv1PZWQSVY/TobZM9HGBWI/AAAAAAAAGsw/nBz8elfRI_w/s1600/imagesCANSD1DK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Tjv1PZWQSVY/TobZM9HGBWI/AAAAAAAAGsw/nBz8elfRI_w/s400/imagesCANSD1DK.jpg\" width=\"307\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Capote has a warped sense of judgement and humor when he suggests that Perry slit the throat and blew off the head of 16 year old Nancy, on moral grounds ( sic!)<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>to prevent Dick from raping her, and thus preserve her honour.&nbsp; Clearly Capote has a intense connection with Perry which did NOT exist with Dick. It is obvious that Truman Capote had ulterior motives in covering the truth.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-1APQ2ojutlo/TobY5AdVDWI/AAAAAAAAGsk/pM2va42g658/s1600/610_capote_intro.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"202\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-1APQ2ojutlo/TobY5AdVDWI/AAAAAAAAGsk/pM2va42g658/s400/610_capote_intro.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Capote may have been unwilling to admit that a much-respected Kansas family could have been murdered as a side effect of a bisexual-gay relationship gone horribly awry, or even to admit that Perry with whom he had a gay relationship was, at the end of the day, responsible for his own actions and crimes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-W7LyMIa3PFA/TobY0_-sGfI/AAAAAAAAGsg/Mgs1CBTuJEY/s1600/240px-Truman_Capote_by_Jack_Mitchell.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-W7LyMIa3PFA/TobY0_-sGfI/AAAAAAAAGsg/Mgs1CBTuJEY/s400/240px-Truman_Capote_by_Jack_Mitchell.jpg\" width=\"276\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">And then Capote croons a white lie, all to show Perry as an angel.&nbsp; &nbsp;Perry told him about how he killed Herb Clutter \u201c I didn\u2019t want to harm the man. I thought he was a very nice gentleman , soft spoken,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>right up to the time I slit his throat!\u201d&nbsp; And then he plods on with his diabolical bullshit. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Perry told him \u201c I placed a cushion under his head before I shot the head off \u201c.&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sniff-&nbsp; <span style=\"font-size: large;\">soo sweeet!!</span> ( with a lisp )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ikJahC_Gu8U/TobYv6CBiHI/AAAAAAAAGsc/wZvAW435mYw/s1600/imagesCAMHPVYR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ikJahC_Gu8U/TobYv6CBiHI/AAAAAAAAGsc/wZvAW435mYw/s400/imagesCAMHPVYR.jpg\" width=\"380\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is obvious that Capote<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>wrote about Perry as if he was really writing about himself rather than the real Perry Smith. Perry was <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>born of two rodeo performers, he had a difficult childhood, served in the military, and became permanently disabled during a motorcycle race. At the same time, he was an avid reader, and liked to draw.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XzeKc1vXYUs/TobcwKRS45I/AAAAAAAAGtY/R2EE89zB9o4/s1600/imagesCA6MX6HX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"237\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XzeKc1vXYUs/TobcwKRS45I/AAAAAAAAGtY/R2EE89zB9o4/s400/imagesCA6MX6HX.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>In researching Smith's back story he discovered disturbing echoes of his own past life: they both had promiscuous, alcoholic mothers and incompetent, largely absent fathers; they were both brought up in foster-homes; they were both ridiculed as children \u2013 Capote for his effeminacy, Smith for his Cherokee blood and his bed wetting. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Capote clearly identified with this \"chunky, misshapen child-man\". <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>In Perry he recognised his shadow, his dark side, the embodiment of his own accumulated angst and hurts. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Though he craved objectivity, Capote found it impossible not to reveal where his sympathies lay. When he claimed that Smith could have stepped right out of one of his stories, it was because Smith resembled Capote's imaginative projection of himself-- they were both outsiders, unacceptable to society -- freaks.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CjvO3wVge3Q/TobakIRahcI/AAAAAAAAGtI/SsyAuVbq22w/s1600/imagesCAOVSTQ1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CjvO3wVge3Q/TobakIRahcI/AAAAAAAAGtI/SsyAuVbq22w/s400/imagesCAOVSTQ1.jpg\" width=\"290\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">The book talks about the brutal 1959 murders of Herbert Clutter, a successful farmer from Holcomb Kansas</span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">, his wife and two of their four children.</span><span lang=\"EN\"> </span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">The elder daughters, Eveanna and Beverly, had moved out of their parents' home ( flown the nest in Yank parlance ) and started their adult lives. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">The two younger children, Nancy, 16, and Kenyon, 15, were high school students living at home. Clutter's wife, Bonnie, a member of the local garden club, had been incapacitated by clinical depression and physical ailments&nbsp;-- basically mid-life syndrome which ALL women pass though.</span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Holcomb<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>was a small, closely knit, god-fearing town located in the west of Kansas State. Comprising principally of blue-collar, middle-class American citizens who lived by the religion, were proud of who they were, and knew most of their fellow-residents in person, the existence of the place was however largely unknown to most Americans. </span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Zx7LDwpi0t0/TobWpt0SfeI/AAAAAAAAGrk/DxbCJXuxug0/s1600/imagesCA9G7758.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"217\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Zx7LDwpi0t0/TobWpt0SfeI/AAAAAAAAGrk/DxbCJXuxug0/s400/imagesCA9G7758.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Herb Clutter, the father, takes out a forty-thousand-dollar life insurance policy, and the family does not lock the doors to their house.&nbsp; Herb Clutter, the father , was the pillar of the town, honest and good, caring for a disabled with, with children as promising, sweet and hopeful as any parent could wish for.. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Kenyon is a boy's boy, not interested in girls yet at fifteen years of age but a talented carpenter. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He was self-conscious, nerdy, and socially awkward.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>He the youngest Clutter, was building a cedar chest to present to his oldest sister. </span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-maM0h9XoILE/TobWcXrCxpI/AAAAAAAAGrg/g0afcsf9lAQ/s1600/imagesCA92T856.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"160\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-maM0h9XoILE/TobWcXrCxpI/AAAAAAAAGrg/g0afcsf9lAQ/s400/imagesCA92T856.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Nancy is the town sweetheart, helpful, generous, attractive, and accomplished. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>A straight-A student and award-winning pie-maker was the most popular girl in her school . She is dating Bobby Rupp, the hunk school basketball star, who is also the last to see the family alive. Mama Bonnie had a problem with depression , and Herbert was very busy with his farming business and did not have much time to tend to her.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Two ex-convicts on parole from the Kansas State Penitentiary, Richard \"Dick\" Hickock and Perry Edward Smith, committed the robbery and murders on November 15, 1959. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>While in jail, a fellow prisoner, Floyd Wells, had told Richard Hickock about a safe at the farmhouse where Herb Clutter supposedly kept enormous of cash. Hickock soon hatched the idea to commit the robbery,&nbsp; and start a new life in Mexico with the moolah. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Hickock described his plan as \"a cinch, the perfect score.\" Hickock later contacted Smith, his former cellmate, about committing the robbery with him. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Even as Herb, the rural wheat growing patriarch, consumes his usual breakfast of an apple and a glass of milk, \"unaware that it would be his last\",<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>and his daughter Nancy lays out her velveteen dress for church, \"the dress in which she was to be buried\", the two ex-cons are racing across the wheat plains of the Midwest in their black Chevrolet sedan, Hickock high on Orange Blossoms, Smith crunching handfuls of aspirin to ease the pin of his grotesquely injured legs.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Smith and Hickock symbolised the feckless, degenerate underbelly of the country, the absolute antithesis of Holcomb's God-fearing and law-abiding citizens<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">After driving 300 miles across the state of Kansas on Saturday, November 14, 1959, Hickock and Smith located the Clutter home and entered while the family slept. </span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mUKgwUBabv0/TobdDEtqIOI/AAAAAAAAGtg/o_V0XG1-0PI/s1600/imagesCACMXY80.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mUKgwUBabv0/TobdDEtqIOI/AAAAAAAAGtg/o_V0XG1-0PI/s400/imagesCACMXY80.jpg\" width=\"258\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">After they roused the family and discovered that there was no money or safe to be found, Smith, notoriously unstable and prone to violent acts in fits of rage, slit Herb Clutter's throat, and then shot him in the head. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Kenyon, then Nancy, and then Bonnie were murdered, each by single shotgun blasts to the head.</span><span lang=\"EN\"> </span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">There were no signs of a struggle, and nothing had been stolen. The telephone lines had been cut. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cyI3vUIvzmk/TobXpgmoY_I/AAAAAAAAGr8/PhCWinXfhoc/s1600/imagesCAR6K3BY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"268\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cyI3vUIvzmk/TobXpgmoY_I/AAAAAAAAGr8/PhCWinXfhoc/s400/imagesCAR6K3BY.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Not a cent is found , or the safe the killers had heard, from a jailbird, which held millions. Perry finds himself chasing a rolling silver dollar on the floor, a souvenir of Clutter's just killed daughter. All they get is 40 dollars and a pair of binoculars.</span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-37_T2-_O9LE/TobX36PGe3I/AAAAAAAAGsA/WZIJ-o_31dI/s1600/imagesCA2S5O88.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"305\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-37_T2-_O9LE/TobX36PGe3I/AAAAAAAAGsA/WZIJ-o_31dI/s400/imagesCA2S5O88.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>The dead bodies of the father, 48-year-old Herbert W. Clutter, was found in the basement with his son, Kenyon, 15. His wife Bonnie, 45, and a daughter, Nancy, 16, were in their beds.</span><span lang=\"EN\"> </span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GQYwjFO7_Ec/TobaUbovt5I/AAAAAAAAGtA/rN7kZ0ZL2q4/s1600/imagesCAZRUQ5I.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"239\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GQYwjFO7_Ec/TobaUbovt5I/AAAAAAAAGtA/rN7kZ0ZL2q4/s320/imagesCAZRUQ5I.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">The crime<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>rocked the nation because it happened in such a small town, where people were presumably more safe than in big cities.</span><span lang=\"EN\"> </span>. The peaceful community was in utter turmoil. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>No one could explain why anyone might have wanted to kill a whole family in Holcomb, a small, poor, rural community in the mid-West Bible belt.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mVYdA6jBjSw/TobabqnjpEI/AAAAAAAAGtE/exMfwReJsgM/s1600/imagesCARML9BW.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"302\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mVYdA6jBjSw/TobabqnjpEI/AAAAAAAAGtE/exMfwReJsgM/s400/imagesCARML9BW.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Richard (\"Dick\") Eugene Hickok and Perry Edward Smith </span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">were identified as suspects and arrested in Las Vegas about six weeks after the crime.</span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Apparently Dick had leaked his plans in jail to someone else, and this man snitched, to curry favour for himself. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The hunt for their killers - parolees Dick Hickock and Perry Smith - mesmerized the American nation, drawing journalists from across the country to this rural outpost on the Kansas prairie.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-OHJfNqSUtsw/TobdXdPqPrI/AAAAAAAAGts/vqT8ZVeiEio/s1600/imagesCAZYG77Z.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"229\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-OHJfNqSUtsw/TobdXdPqPrI/AAAAAAAAGts/vqT8ZVeiEio/s400/imagesCAZYG77Z.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Their killers came from as different a world as you could find in rural America at the time. Perry Smith's family was broken and violent. He'd lost two siblings to suicide, and a parent to alcoholism. Half-Cherokee, half-Irish, Smith had a \"runty\" build, thanks to a motorcycle accident that left him with disfigured legs and an addiction to dry chewing painkilling aspirin and glorified daydreams.&nbsp; </span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Dick Hickock's ambitions were slightly less delusional; he just wanted to take the money and run off somewhere he wouldn't be found.&nbsp; Hickock was also scarred,&nbsp; A car accident had put an unnerving asymmetry into his otherwise handsome face. Ever since his face got disfigured he is a completely different person. Hickock's family was poor but relatively stable They pleaded temporary insanity at the trial, but local GPs evaluated the accused and pronounced them sane. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">After reading a short newspaper account of the killings, Truman Capote decided to make the 1,700km journey from his home in New York to Holcomb to chronicle the impact of terrible violence on a small community. He takes his Alabama childhood friend Harper Lee along. They arrive in time for the funeral. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yIssDqvhRzs/TobdStL8xvI/AAAAAAAAGto/G8bRUi_tusg/s1600/untitlednhy.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yIssDqvhRzs/TobdStL8xvI/AAAAAAAAGto/G8bRUi_tusg/s400/untitlednhy.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Harper Lee, who within a few months will win a Pulitzer Prize and achieve fame of her own as the author of runaway best seller<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>\"To Kill a Mockingbird.\". This book&nbsp;will soon sell a mindboggling 30 million copies,.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The book deals with the issues of racism that were observed by her, as a child in her hometown of Monroeville, Alabama .</span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LvS41IQJ9Ls/TobdJ1bGWqI/AAAAAAAAGtk/2OcfwcQwp4M/s1600/imagesCAY398E7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LvS41IQJ9Ls/TobdJ1bGWqI/AAAAAAAAGtk/2OcfwcQwp4M/s400/imagesCAY398E7.jpg\" width=\"300\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Capote's first few days in town were difficult. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Everyone gave the weird 5 feet 3 inches , squeaky voiced , high strung Truman Capote the royal brush-off.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Harper Lee was crucial in overcoming the initial hostility. She had agreed to accompany Capote to act as what he called his \"assistant researchist\".&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Her affable southern manner \u2013 she <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>made for a much happier connection with the plain-spoken rustic inhabitants of Holcomb.&nbsp; Rupp recalls that in the one interview he granted Capote, most of the questions were asked by Harper Lee, so much so that \"sometimes I wonder who really wrote that book\". </span><span lang=\"EN\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;Harper</span></span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"> sort of managed Truman, acting as his guardian or mother hen. She broke the ice for him.</span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Et4DWN548Gw/TobYch6gC0I/AAAAAAAAGsU/EYZFfuhxWSA/s1600/imagesCAVQQ2RD.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"295\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Et4DWN548Gw/TobYch6gC0I/AAAAAAAAGsU/EYZFfuhxWSA/s400/imagesCAVQQ2RD.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">After five years on death row, Smith and Hickock aged 36 and 33, were executed by hanging by their necks , just after midnight on April 14, 1965, in Lansing, Kansas, at the Kansas State Penitentiary (now known as Lansing Correctional Facility).</span><span lang=\"EN\"> <span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large; mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">It was only six years after he started writing , when the two drifters were executed&nbsp;, that Capote would finish his book</span>. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN;\">The gallows from which they were hanged now forms part of the collections of the Kansas State Historical Society. </span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bNBK78Mu4iA/TobYkTdqf6I/AAAAAAAAGsY/-eQvHcow4_U/s1600/imagesCAKJPRJS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"258\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bNBK78Mu4iA/TobYkTdqf6I/AAAAAAAAGsY/-eQvHcow4_U/s400/imagesCAKJPRJS.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Today, tourists from as far as Japan come in droves to Holcomb, to get the feel of the place \u2013nay\u2014 for a pilgrimage of sorts. . They visit the cemetery , where there are three neat tombstones, all bearing the date 1959: Herb and Bonnie together in the centre, Kenyon on the right and Nancy to the left. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4twDbjLFC8M/TobW4oZBKhI/AAAAAAAAGro/avFvef-LptY/s1600/imagesCAYEQ17C.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"278\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4twDbjLFC8M/TobW4oZBKhI/AAAAAAAAGro/avFvef-LptY/s400/imagesCAYEQ17C.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The River Valley farm <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>still looks on the exterior largely as he described it. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It now belongs to its third set of owners since the Clutters, the Maders.&nbsp;&nbsp; They used to give tours of the property but grew so hot and bothered by the endless inquisitive stream of \u201cIn Cold Blood pilgrims\u201d that they posted the \"NYET\" sign. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tmgvROxRPGE/TobXBi--9QI/AAAAAAAAGrs/WzpUJSBelCo/s1600/VB.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"256\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tmgvROxRPGE/TobXBi--9QI/AAAAAAAAGrs/WzpUJSBelCo/s400/VB.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In Garden City, the Wheat Lands motel where Capote and Harper Lee stayed, is still there, though a photo of Capote posing in front of the building has been stolen from the foyer. The courthouse where Smith and Hickock were put on trial still stands as imposing as it was then. Holcomb, population 270 in 1959, has grown tenfold and is now dominated by one of the world's largest meat-packing factories<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IgR96w-jCQI/TobYS7LoePI/AAAAAAAAGsQ/Lr0c5jRTjps/s1600/imagesCAOZGZS4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"317\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IgR96w-jCQI/TobYS7LoePI/AAAAAAAAGsQ/Lr0c5jRTjps/s400/imagesCAOZGZS4.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nancy\u2019s friend Bob Rupp,who was her last date as a teenager upset<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>\"They made a tremendous amount of money off our great tragedy\". </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WKhRSSMsR-4/TobbOaB9EHI/AAAAAAAAGtQ/4612WS-gDwU/s1600/imagesCAKAFFWV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WKhRSSMsR-4/TobbOaB9EHI/AAAAAAAAGtQ/4612WS-gDwU/s400/imagesCAKAFFWV.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The book has been loathed and reviled in its birthplace by residents because of its recreation of events (as per Perry cum Capote's morbid delusions ) that never happened, &nbsp;and what they say is commercial exploitation of the victims. The subsequent Hollywood movies have also been very unpopular here. The town is all American with the distinctive spirit of revenge and the cowboy posse mentality to catch them outlaws.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CHQe7tWqBDM/TobYMY6FBsI/AAAAAAAAGsM/7DUlPT9MwMQ/s1600/imagesCAURX892.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"263\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CHQe7tWqBDM/TobYMY6FBsI/AAAAAAAAGsM/7DUlPT9MwMQ/s400/imagesCAURX892.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"In cold blood\" vividly portrays how the nice American dream turns into the scary American nightmare by juxtaposing and dovetailing the lives and values of the Clutters and those of the killers. Truman Capote elaborates the&nbsp;starkness of &nbsp;the split image and deep doubleness of American life. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RSWB8Y2kBqI/TobXgv4qhyI/AAAAAAAAGr4/kYjs5FPOMG4/s1600/imagesCADP98VI.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RSWB8Y2kBqI/TobXgv4qhyI/AAAAAAAAGr4/kYjs5FPOMG4/s400/imagesCADP98VI.jpg\" width=\"232\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The two criminals with questionable mental dispositions have been brought forth with chilling effect, with all their hopes, aspirations, nuances, onion layers, secret desires, flaws, pathological tendencies, and criminal inclinations.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TMcrH-vnZkk/TobX_GasnMI/AAAAAAAAGsE/DWzK-py77Gw/s1600/imagesCAH6VONV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TMcrH-vnZkk/TobX_GasnMI/AAAAAAAAGsE/DWzK-py77Gw/s400/imagesCAH6VONV.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; </span>2-Propenic Acid,2-Propenoic Acid, Propenoic Acid, Vinyl Formic Acid.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; Acrylic acid monomer can be used in latex to prevent coagulation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;
