text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">AH/ 28C<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">DH/ 25C<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Marpol cat/ Y<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Vapor pressure 20C (mmHg)/ 3.10<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Vapor pressure 46C (psia)/ 0.4<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Vapor density (air =1.0)/ 2.48<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Viscosity/ 1.30 mPas<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Solubility in water/ complete<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Low surface tension. Cleaning chemicals not required..<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Flammable vapors, combustible liquid. Vapors can flow along surfaces to distant ignition sources and flash back.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Presents no special fire or explosion hazard because of its relatively high flash point and low vapor pressure. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Poisonous gases may be produced in a fire.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">FP/ 50C<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">AIT/ 438C<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Flammable limits: 2.4 LEL to 8.02 UEL<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Does not react with water.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Good cargo before the next wall wash cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Alcohol resistant foam used to combat fires. Carbon monoxide and carbon di oxide may form when heated to decomposition.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">A fire involving a spill on tank deck could be extinguished with dry chemical or foam. Wear full protective clothing, eye protection and self-contained breathing apparatus<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Destructive to mucous membranes and upper respiratory tract.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">May be fatal as a result of spasm, inflammation and edemaof the larynx and bronchi, chemical pneumonitis and pulmonary odema. Asphyxia may occur due to edema of the glottis.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Fairly severe skin irritants, usually causing pain and second degree bums after a few minutes contact<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Threshold limit value/TWA/10 ppm (skin)<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Acrylic acid, when in contact with skin or eyes, may result in a bum upon short contact. Vapor may present an inhalation hazard from single exposures; irritating to eyes, nose and throat<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Vapors are capable of causing definite skin or eye irritation, nasal irritation and lachrymation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">STEL/ 0.5 ppm.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If contact with skin or eye occurs, immediately flush with plenty of water for at least 15 minutes. Get medical attention promptly. Immediately remove contaminated clothing and shoes.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Polymerizes readily. Should be inhibited to insure safety and stability during storage and handling. Light promotes polymerization once started.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Severely corrodes iron and steel. Glass, low carbon content stainless steel and high purity aluminum are recommended.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">No inerting by nitrogen must be done as stabilizer is oxygen dependant.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">USCG compatibility chart/4\u2014see exceptions<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Incompatible with strong oxidizing agents.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If possible, wear rubber gloves, face shield, protective clothing. Body shield and self-contained breathing apparatus should be available<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If leak on cargo transfer system, stop the transfer and empty the line system. Flush contaminated area with a weak caustic soda solution (10%), then flush the area with large quantities of water<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Acrylic Acid is an unstable product when not inhibited. The ester grade (technical grade) covered by this manual is relatively stable when properly inhibited.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Acrylic Acid is regulated for bulk transportation by the IMO, BCH and IBC codes. Following is the summary of the codes' minimum requirements:<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Pollution category/D (old) \u2014NEW Y<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Fire protection/ Alcohol resistant foam<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LHPL6TB00Bk/ToVpgY3Y7ZI/AAAAAAAAGp8/tKVVmjO0OLw/s1600/XXC.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LHPL6TB00Bk/ToVpgY3Y7ZI/AAAAAAAAGp8/tKVVmjO0OLw/s1600/XXC.png\" /></span></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">ARRANGEMENTS<u> </u><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Establish method for heating the cargo. Thermal oil, hot water, and/or adjacent heating is to be used. The safest way is to use adjacent heat by filling up fresh water ( not salt water) in an adjacent ballast tank and maintaining its temperature &lt;30 deg C.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Do not use heating systems to thaw a solidified monomer.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For the transportation, and in case of rapid temperature increase ensure to have prepared plans to abandon the cargo overboard if so is required to protect the safety of crew and ship.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Stowage is to be arranged so that tanks are not filled to more than 90% full.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The cargo should never be allowed to freeze (MP 12-14C) as when cargo is remelted there is great risk of violent polymerization.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">EQUIPMENT<u><o:p></o:p></u></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Since temperature measurement and records are a bone of contention,--ensure<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Tanks to be loaded need a minimum of two temperature sensors in each tank with high and low temperature alarms. Ullages need to be arranged accordingly so that two sensors are in contact with the cargo during the voyage in each tank. High temperature alarm to be set at 35C and low temperature alarm to be set at 18C.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">PREPARATION FOR LOADING<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The tank must be dry, and chlorides &lt; 2ppm.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Check heating coils for leaks (follow procedure for non-destructive pressure testing of heating coils). Steam coils to be blown dry and blanked off if using AH.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Purge the Framo pump and check for seal tightness (use air).<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Prepare 10% caustic soda solution for neutralization of spills.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Ensure that all handling personnel are using acid resistant protective gear.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Have respiratory apparatus, eye wash, and emergency showers ready for use.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Use splash couplings at manifold.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Adjacent tanks or ballast spaces must not contain cargo or ballast with a temperature less than 18C at any time during the loading or voyage.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If you are loading in a cold place inject warm air into the pipelines to be used for loading to keep temperature at 20C. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">LOADING</span></u><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The cargo should be loaded with a temperature range of 18/28C.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">No samples to be retained on board.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">An inhibitor certificate must be obtained. The inhibitor used is usually Hydroquinone. Acrylic acid vapor contains no inhibitor. So the condensate may polymerise inside the PV stack. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">During loading cargo temperature must be checked and logged every 30 minutes.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">First foot sample stop will be given by ship.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The first 24 hours after loading the cargo temperature must be checked and logged every 2 hours.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">AFTER LOADING<o:p></o:p></span></span></u></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Samples must be drawn from top , middle and bottom levels of the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 9pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For line clearing use air, do not use nitrogen as the inhibitor stabilizing the cargo is oxygen dependent.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 9pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">All equipment used for Acrylic Acid loading must be thoroughly cleaned before stowed away. Cargo hoses should be flushed with warm (35-40C) water and steamed before stowed away.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"FR1\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-weight: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">VOYAGE<o:p></o:p></span></span></u></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The cargo temperatures must be monitored every four hours (00-04-08-12-16-20) and the results recorded in the \"Cargo Temperature Log.\".<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The Log should contain the following information\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Outside temperature<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Sea water temperature<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">AH by FW temperature<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Top middle bottom cargo temperatures<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Weather<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The cargo temperature log must be Emailed every 24 hrs to the charterers and operator.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If the temperature falls below 18C, introduce heat using thermal oil/hot water or adjacent tank heating system. Heating coils surface temperature must not exceed 35C.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If the temperature continues to either decrease or increase to 16C or 34C respectively, urgently notify<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the Chemical operator-- if the temperature change is not due to the corresponding ambient temperatures. If the temperature rises to 35C read <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Jettison Procedures and be fore warned.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">PRE-DISCHARGE ARRANGEMENTS<o:p></o:p></span></span></u></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Prepare and use only clean, dry hoses.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Use acid spray shields at manifold flanges.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">10% caustic soda solution can be used for neutralization of spills<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 13pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">All handling personnel should wear PPE..<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">DISCHARGE</span></u><u><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></u></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The cargo should preferably be discharged at a temperature between 18C and 28C.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 12pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">During discharge cargo temperature must be checked and logged every 30 minutes.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><u>TANK CLEANING<o:p></o:p></u></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">All tanks need to be stripped as per P&amp;A Manual. Shortly after discharge all tanks are to be rinsed with clean ambient (MP--- 12C + 10C = 22C ) fresh water (not seawater or river water) to dilute any remaining acid. </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">This mixture is to remain in the tank until it is cleaned at sea (salt water ok) as per Marpol Regulations. Alternatively this fresh water/acid mixture may be transferred into another clean SS tank or empty (rinsed) acid tank so the tank may be cleaned in port. </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Under no circumstances is the fresh water/acid mixture to be mixed with any other slops onboard (except for other Acrylic Acid slops.) After initial rinsing and transfer of slops the Acrylic Acid tank may be cleaned in port with salt or channel water collecting slops onboard along with any other compatible slops.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">This cargo can polymerize violently if contaminated or if exposed to freezing (12-14C) or excessive heat (45C) so utmost care needs to be taken when handling or cleaning from this cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If heating coils have not been used for heating, remove blinds and thoroughly flush the coils with fresh water and check pH is 7..<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Steam line systems, ensure to flush at all drain cocks and plugs.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Dry tank and lines.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If there are any black marks it can be removed by phosphoric acid.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">SLOP DISPOSAL AND ARRANGEMENTS <o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The slops are to be disposed according to:<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Regulations for control of pollution by noxious liquid substances in bulk, IMO, MARPOL Annex II and, when it is necessary to dispose slops to shore reception facilities, the ship must report estimated quantities to the Ship Operator and the local agent. Before mixing compatible slop residues or slops and cleaning agents consult the local agent.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kruss4JZw2E/ToVpmFXNCjI/AAAAAAAAGqA/SqgWLD5F9no/s1600/SER.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kruss4JZw2E/ToVpmFXNCjI/AAAAAAAAGqA/SqgWLD5F9no/s1600/SER.png\" /></span></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;
